function newUI(ship,id,xPos,yPos,value,shortcut){
  ship.setUIComponent({
    id:shortcut,
    position:[xPos,yPos,2.5,4.5],
    clickable: true,
    shortcut: "",
    visible: true,
    components: [
      { type: "text",position:[0,0,100,100],value:shortcut,color:"rgba(0, 234, 0, 1)"},
    ]
  });
  ship.setUIComponent({
    id:id,
    position:[xPos,yPos,18,4.5],
    clickable: true,
    shortcut: shortcut,
    visible: true,
    components: [
      { type:  "box",position:[0,0,100,100],fill:"rgba(68, 85, 102, 0)",stroke:"rgba(0, 234, 0, 1)",width:4},
      { type: "text",position:[0,0,100,95],value:value,color:"rgba(0, 234, 0, 1)"},
    ]
  });
}

    visible: true,
    components: [
      { type: "text",position:[0,0,100,100],value:shortcut,color:"rgba(255, 0, 0, 1)"},
    ]
  });
  setTimeout( () => {
    ship.setUIComponent({
      id:id,
      position:[xPos,yPos,18,4.5],
      clickable: true,
      shortcut: shortcut,
      visible: true,
      components: [
        { type:  "box",position:[0,0,100,100],fill:"rgba(68, 85, 102, 0)",stroke:"rgba(0, 255, 0, 1)",width:4},
        { type: "text",position:[0,0,100,95],value:value,color:"rgba(0, 255, 0, 1)"},
      ]
    });
    ship.setUIComponent({
      id:shortcut,
      position:[xPos,yPos,2.5,4.5],
      clickable: true,
      shortcut: "",
      visible: true,
      components: [
        { type: "text",position:[0,0,100,100],value:shortcut,color:"rgba(0, 255, 0, 1)"},
      ]
    });
  }, 15000);
}

function gameWon(name){
  for(s=0;s<game.ships.length;s++){
    game.ships[s].setUIComponent({
      id:"game_won",
      position:[25,20,50,50],
      clickable: false,
      shortcut: "",
      visible: true,
      components: [
        { type: "text",position:[0,0,100,100],value:name+" has won!",color:"rgba(0, 255, 0, 1)"},
      ]
    });
  }
  setTimeout( () => {
    for(s=0;s<game.ships.length;s++){
      game.ships[s].setUIComponent({
        id:"game_won",
        visible: false
      });
    }
  }, 5000);
  echo("game has been won");
}

//ability functions
function hyperSpeed(ship){
  if (ship.custom.hyper && ship.type != 101){
    ship.custom.hyper = false;
    ship.set({type:702});
    setTimeout( () => {
    ship.set({type:701});
    }, 400);
            
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.custom.hyper = true;
    }, 15000);
  }
}

function missileSwarm(ship){
  if (ship.custom.swarm && ship.type != 101){
    ship.custom.swarm = false;
    swarmId = ship.id;
    spamStop = false;
    setTimeout( () => {
      spamStop = true;
    }, 8000);
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.custom.swarm = true;
    }, 15000);
  }
}

function absoluteKun(ship){
  if (ship.custom.kun && ship.type != 101){
    ship.custom.kun = false;
    ship.set({type:703});
    setTimeout( () => {
    ship.set({type:701});
    }, 4500);
            
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.custom.kun = true;
    }, 15000);
  }
}

function burstHeal(ship){
  if (ship.custom.heal && ship.type != 101){
    ship.custom.heal = false;
    ship.set({shield:ship.shield+14000});
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.custom.heal = true;
    }, 15000);
  }
}

function overdrive(ship){
  if (ship.custom.over && ship.type != 101){
    ship.custom.over = false;
    ship.set({type:704});
    setTimeout( () => {
    ship.set({type:701});
    }, 6000);
            
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.custom.over = true;
    }, 15000);
  }
}

function Deathray(ship){
  if (ship.custom.ray && ship.type != 101){
    ship.custom.ray = false;
    ship.set({type:705,generator:10000});
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.set({type:701});
    }, 5000);
            
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.custom.ray = true;
    }, 15000);
  }
}

function Diarrhea(ship){
  if (ship.custom.diarrhea && ship.type != 101){
    ship.custom.diarrhea = false;
    ship.set({type:706,generator:10000});
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.set({type:701});
    }, 5000);
            
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.custom.diarrhea = true;
    }, 15000);
  }
}
function laserWave(ship){
  if(ship.custom.wave && ship.type != 101){
    ship.custom.wave = false;
    ship.set({type:707,generator:30000});
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.set({type:701});
    }, 3500);
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.custom.wave = true;
    }, 15000);
  }
}

    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.set({type:701});

  if(ship.custom.mega && ship.type != 101){
    ship.custom.mega = false;
    ship.set({type:709,generator:10000});
    setTimeout( () => {
      ship.set({type:701});

this.options = {
  root_mode: "",
  map_size: 60,
  custom_map: map,
  starting_ship:701,
  ships:ships,
  reset_tree: true,
  asteroids_strength: 1000000,
  starting_ship_maxed: true,
  crystal_value: 5,
  weapons_store: false,
  radar_zoom: 1.8,
  max_level: 7,
  max_tier_lives: 0,
  map_name: "Mothership-Mayhem"
  
};

this.tick = function(game,ship) {
  if (spamStop === false){
    if (game.step%15 === 0) {
    game.collectibles.splice(0, game.collectibles.length);
    for (let ship of game.ships) {
      if (ship.id === swarmId) {
        ship.emptyWeapons();
        game.addCollectible({
          code: 11,
          x: ship.x,
          y: ship.y
        });
      }
    }
    }
  }
  //teleporters
  for(let ship of game.ships){
    if(Math.sqrt(Math.pow(ship.x, 2) + Math.pow(ship.y, 2) >= 17000)){
      ship.set({vx:ship.vx*-1,vy:ship.vy*-1,x:ship.x*0.99,y:ship.y*0.99});
    }
  }
};


this.event = function(event, game) {
  switch (event.name) {
    case "ship_spawned":
      if(!event.ship.custom.respawn){
        playersLeft.push(event.ship.id);
      }
      echo(playersLeft);
      //UI components
      newUI(event.ship,"hyper_speed",1,30,"Hyperspeed","1");
      newUI(event.ship,"missile_swarm",1,35,"Missile-Spam","2");
      newUI(event.ship,"absolute_kun",1,40,"Absolute-Kun","3");
      newUI(event.ship,"burst_heal",1,45,"Burst-Heal","4");
      newUI(event.ship,"over_drive",1,50,"Overdrive","5");
      newUI(event.ship,"death_ray",1,55,"Deathray","6");
      newUI(event.ship,"diarrhea_spurt",1,60,"Diarrhea","7");
      newUI(event.ship,"laser_wave",1,65,"Laser-Wave","8");
      newUI(event.ship,"mini_ship",1,70,"Mini-Ship","9");
      newUI(event.ship,"mega_pulse",1,75,"Mega-Pulse","0");
      //setting new player's ablility ready true
      event.ship.custom.hyper = true;
      event.ship.custom.swarm = true;
      event.ship.custom.kun = true;
      event.ship.custom.heal = true;
      event.ship.custom.over = true;
      event.ship.custom.ray = true;
      event.ship.custom.diarrhea = true;
      event.ship.custom.wave = true;
      event.ship.custom.mini = true;
      event.ship.custom.mega = true;
      //welcome message and instructions
      event.ship.set({crystals:980, shield:50000});
      if(!event.ship.custom.respawn){
        event.ship.instructorSays("Welcome, commander, to Mothership Mayhem!","Kan");
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("Your mothership has been equiped with 10 ability modules, each of which can be used once every 15 seconds.","Kan");
      }, 750);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("1 - Hyperspeed","Kan");
      }, 5750);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("2 - Missile-Spam","Kan");
      }, 8250);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("3 - Absolute-Kuntrol","Kan");
      }, 11250);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("4 - Burst-Heal","Kan");
      }, 14750);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("5 - Overdrive. I have upgraded this module so that it no longer damages your own ship while being used.","Kan");
      }, 16750);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("6 - Deathray","Kan");
      }, 19750);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("7 - Diarrhea. Your mothership ate some moldy cheese.","Kan");
      }, 21750);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("8 - Laser-Wave","Kan");
      }, 24750);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("9 - Mini-Ship. It's like your ship, but mini.","Kan");
      }, 26750);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("10 - Mega-Pulse. 10,000 damage in one big pulse","Kan");
      }, 29750);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("Be sure to utilise your burst heal. You'll be killed pretty quickly if you don't.","Kan");
      }, 33750);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.instructorSays("Good luck commander!","Kan");
      }, 35750);
      setTimeout( () => {
        event.ship.hideInstructor();
      }, 38750);
      }
      break;
    case "ui_component_clicked":
      switch (event.id) {
        
        case "hyper_speed":
          hyperSpeed(event.ship);
          //ship,id,xPos,yPos,shortcut,value
          cooldownUI(event.ship,"hyper_speed",1,30,"1","Hyperspeed");
          break;
          
        case "missile_swarm":
          missileSwarm(event.ship);
          cooldownUI(event.ship,"missile_swarm",1,35,"2","Missile-Spam");
          break;
          
        case "absolute_kun":
          absoluteKun(event.ship);
          cooldownUI(event.ship,"absolute_kun",1,40,"3","Absolute-Kun");
          break;
          
        case "burst_heal":
          burstHeal(event.ship);
          cooldownUI(event.ship,"burst_heal",1,45,"4","Burst-Heal");
          break;
          
        case "over_drive":
          overdrive(event.ship);
          cooldownUI(event.ship,"over_drive",1,50,"5","Overdrive");
          break;
        
        case "death_ray":
          Deathray(event.ship);
          cooldownUI(event.ship,"death_ray",1,55,"6","Deathray");
          break;
          
        case "diarrhea_spurt":
          Diarrhea(event.ship);
          cooldownUI(event.ship,"diarrhea_spurt",1,60,"7","Diarrhea");
          break;
        
        case "laser_wave":
          laserWave(event.ship);
          cooldownUI(event.ship,"laser_wave",1,65,"8","Laser-Wave");
          break;
        
        case "mini_ship":
          miniShip(event.ship);
          cooldownUI(event.ship,"mini_ship",1,70,"9","Mini-Ship");
          break;
          
        case "mega_pulse":
          megaPulse(event.ship);
          cooldownUI(event.ship,"mega_pulse",1,75,"0","Mega-Pulse");
          break;
          
        
      }
      break;
    case "ship_destroyed":
      event.ship.custom.respawn = true;
      //set killed ship to spectator and remove it's id from playersLeft
      event.ship.intermission({"Rank":game.ships.length});
      event.ship.set({type:101,collider:false});
      playersLeft.splice(playersLeft.indexOf(event.ship.id),1);
      echo(playersLeft);
      //check if there is only one mothership left, and run gameWon if there is
      if(playersLeft.length === 1){
        gameWon(game.findShip(playersLeft[0]).name);
        //wait 4.5 seconds then clear playersLeft, then add all ids and set players with motherships
        setTimeout( () => {
          playersLeft = [];
          echo(playersLeft+" after clear");
          for(s=0;s<game.ships.length;s++){
            game.ships[s].set({type:701,collider:true});
            playersLeft.push(game.ships[s].id);
            echo(playersLeft+" after reset");
          }
        }, 4500);
      }
      break;
  }
};
